# Exercise 1: Basic searching and filtering

from pymongo import MongoClient

client = MongoClient("mongodb+srv://stephen01n:m1Lg6G6Xqk276eCm@cluster0.qjffu.mongodb.net/?retryWrites=true&w=majority&appName=Cluster0v")
db = client.sample_mflix
collection = db.movies

# Task 1
action_movie = collection.find_one({"genres": "Action"})
print("Task 1", action_movie)

# Task 2
movies_after_2000 = collection.find({"year": {"$gt": 2000}}).limit(5)
print("Task 2")
for movie in movies_after_2000:
    print(movie)

# Task 3:
high_rated_movies = collection.find({"imdb.rating": {"$gt": 8.5}}).limit(5)
print("Task 3")
for movie in high_rated_movies:
    print(movie)

# Task 4
action_adventure_movies = collection.find({"genres": {"$all": ["Action", "Adventure"]}}).limit(5)
print("Task 4")
for movie in action_adventure_movies:
    print(movie)

# Exercise 2: Sorting results

# task 1
sorted_comedy_movies = collection.find({"genres": "Comedy"}).sort("imdb.rating", -1).limit(5)
print("Task 1: Sorted Comedy Movies")
for movie in sorted_comedy_movies:
    print(movie)

# task 2
sorted_drama_movies = collection.find({"genres": "Drama"}).sort("year", 1).limit(5)
print("Task 2: Sorted Drama Movies")
for movie in sorted_drama_movies:
    print(movie)

# exercise 3: aggregation pipeline

# task 1
avg_rating_by_genre = collection.aggregate([
    {"$unwind": "$genres"},
    {"$group": {"_id": "$genres", "avg_rating": {"$avg": "$imdb.rating"}}},
    {"$sort": {"avg_rating": -1}},
    {"$limit": 5}
])
print("Task 1: Top 5 Genres by Average IMDb Rating")
for genre in avg_rating_by_genre:
    print(genre)

# task 2
top_directors = collection.aggregate([
    {"$group": {"_id": "$directors", "avg_rating": {"$avg": "$imdb.rating"}}},
    {"$sort": {"avg_rating": -1}},
    {"$limit": 5}
])
print("Task 2: Top 5 Directors by Average IMDb Rating")
for director in top_directors:
    print(director)

# task 3
movies_per_year = collection.aggregate([
    {"$group": {"_id": "$year", "total_movies": {"$sum": 1}}},
    {"$sort": {"_id": 1}}
])
print("Task 3: Total Number of Movies Released Each Year")
for year in movies_per_year:
    print(year)

# task 1

# task 2

# task 3
collection.delete_many({"year": {"$lt": 1950}})

from pymongo import MongoClient

# Find movies with 'love' in the title
love_movies = collection.find({"$text": {"$search": "love"}})
print("Movies with 'love' in the title:")
for movie in love_movies:
    print(movie)  # Ensure this line is indented

# Task 2: Text search across title and plot, sorted by IMDb rating
war_movies = collection.find({"$text": {"$search": "war"}}).sort("imdb.rating", -1).limit(5)
print("Top 5 movies with 'war' in the title or plot, sorted by IMDb rating:")
for movie in war_movies:
    print(movie)  # Ensure this line is indented

# Exercise 6: Combining Multiple Queries (Bonus Exercise)
action_high_rated_movies = collection.find({"genres": "Action", "imdb.rating": {"$gt": 8}}).sort("year", -1)
print("Action movies with IMDb rating greater than 8, sorted by release year (descending):")
for movie in action_high_rated_movies:
    print(movie)

nolan_movies = collection.find({"directors": "Christopher Nolan", "imdb.rating": {"$gt": 8}}).sort("imdb.rating", -1).limit(3)
print("Top 3 Christopher Nolan movies with IMDb rating greater than 8, sorted by rating:")
for movie in nolan_movies:
    print(movie)
